NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

NOTICE
I Komandur Ramanratnam Ashok Adopeted OM PRAKASH alias KOMANDUR ASHOK ANIRUDH under Miscellaneous
Petition No. 111 of 2000 in the Matter of the Hindu Adoption Act, 1956 in the Bombay City Civil Court.
The Hounarable Court has passed an order to this effect on 19th day of August 2000 that OM PARKASH alias
KOMANDUR ASHOK ANIRUDH Legally Adopted Child of Komandur Ramaratnam Ashok.
The name of the minor child OM PRAKASH alias KOMANDUR ASHOK ANIRUDH (D.O.B. 13/1/2000) shall be known
as ANIRUDH ASHOK.
L7G, Bharathidasan Colony,
K.K. Nagar,
Chennai-600 078,
1-8-2014.

KOMANDUR RAMARATNAM ASHOK.
